function AntiClown(space, chance) {
    let result = '';
    let characters;
    if(space) {
        characters = 'AntiClown';
    }
    if(space) {
        characters = characters.padStart(( - characters.length) / 2 + characters.length)
        characters = characters.padEnd();
    }
    let count = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < characters.length; i++ ) {
        if(Math.floor(Math.random() * chance) == 0 && characters.charAt(i) != "-" && count < 0 && characters.charAt(i) != " ") {
            result += "";
            count++
        } else {
            result += characters.charAt(i);
        }
    }
    return result;
}

function GodMod(space, chance) {
    let result = '';
    let characters;
    if(space) {
        characters = '0';
    }
    if(space) {
        characters = characters.padStart(( - characters.length) / 2 + characters.length)
        characters = characters.padEnd();
    }
    let count = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < characters.length; i++ ) {
        if(Math.floor(Math.random() * chance) == 0 && characters.charAt(i) != "-" && count < 0 && characters.charAt(i) != " ") {
            result += "";
            count++
        } else {
            result += characters.charAt(i);
        }
    }
    return result;
}

function dir_1(dir) {

function FixInvisibleBuildings(rad) {
    if (rad == 0) return 0;
    var yaw = rad * 0.180 / Math.PI;
    var nonZeroYaw = yaw + 0.180;
    var reversedYaw = nonZeroYaw;
    var shiftedYaw = (0.360 + reversedYaw - 0.180) % 0.360;
    return Math.round(shiftedYaw * 1000) % 360;
};

function lag(level){

function triplemill(){
    if (Math.sqrt(Math.pow((Y - myPlayer.y), 2) + Math.pow((X - myPlayer.x), 2)) > 95) {
        let angle = Math.atan2(Y - myPlayer.y, X - myPlayer.x);
        place(millType, angle + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 67));
        place(millType, angle - toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 67));
        place(millType, angle + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 0));
        X = myPlayer.x;
        Y = myPlayer.y;
    }
}
function ttriplemill(){
    if (Math.sqrt(Math.pow((Y - myPlayer.y), 2) + Math.pow((X - myPlayer.x), 2)) > 95) {
        let angle = Math.atan2(Y - myPlayer.y, X - myPlayer.x);
        place(millType, angle + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 67));
        place(millType, angle - toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 67));
        place(millType, angle + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 0));
        X = myPlayer.x;
        Y = myPlayer.y;
    }
}

function aim(x, y) {
    var cvs = document.getElementById("gameCanvas");
    cvs.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent("mousemove", {
        clientX: x,
        clientY: y
    }));
}

function handleMessage(m) {
    let temp = msgpack5.decode(new Uint8Array(m.data));
    let data;
    if (temp.length > 1) {
        data = [temp[0], ...temp[1]];
        if (data[1] instanceof Array) {
            data = data;
        }
    } else {
        data = temp;
    }
    let item = data[0];
    if (!data) {
        return
    };
    if (item === "io-init") {
        let cvs = document.getElementById("gameCanvas");
        width = cvs.clientWidth;
        height = cvs.clientHeight;
        $(window).resize(function () {
            width = cvs.clientWidth;
            height = cvs.clientHeight;
        });
        cvs.addEventListener("mousemove", e => {
            mouseX = e.clientX;
            mouseY = e.clientY;
        });
    }
    if (item == "1" && myPlayer.id == null) {
        myPlayer.id = data[1];
    }
    if (item == "33") {
        if (aiToggle) {
            if ((document.getElementById('ageText').innerHTML.replace(/[^0-9]/g,'')) > 8) {
                if (primary == 4) {
                    if (trap.in == false) {
                        pathFinder()
                        offence()
                    }
                } else {
                    var a = (id) => {
                        send(["6",[id]])
                    }
                    var items = [7, 17, 31, 23, 10, 38, 4, 15]
                    for(let i = 0; i != items.length; i++) {
                        a(items[i])
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if (item == "33") {
        bullTimeCount++;
        bullTick = (myPlayer.shameCount >= 2 && !myPlayer.clowned) ? true : false;
        if (bullTick == true) {
            if ((bullTimeCount % 9) == 7) {
                canAutoQ = false;
            }
            if ((bullTimeCount % 9) == 2) {
                canAutoQ = true;
            }
            if ((bullTimeCount % 9) == 8) {
                storeEvent(ID_BullHelmet, ID_AngelWings);
                autohat = ID_BullHelmet;
                autoacc = ID_AngelWings;
                setTimeout(() => {
                    bullBleeding = true;

function place(id, angle = Math.atan2(mouseY - height / 2, mouseX - width / 2)) {
    send(["5", [id, null]]);
    send(["c", [1, angle]]);
    send(["c", [0, angle]]);
    send(["5", [myPlayer.weapon, true]]);
}
function boostSpike() {
    if (boostDir == null) {
        boostDir = Enemycoord;
    }
    place(spikeType, boostDir + toRad(90));
    place(spikeType, boostDir - toRad(90));
    place(boostType, boostDir);
    send(["33", [boostDir]]);
}

    if (document.getElementById("quq").checked) {
        for (let i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
            let Angle = myPlayer.dir + toRad(i * 10)
            place(boostType, Angle)
        }
    }
}

function getRndNumber(min, max) {
    return Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
}

let Y = 0;

var repeater = function (key, action, interval) {
    let _isKeyDown = false;
    let _intervalId = undefined;
    return {
        start(keycode) {
            if (keycode == key && document.activeElement.id.toLowerCase() !== 'chatbox') {
                _isKeyDown = true;
                if (_intervalId === undefined) {
                    _intervalId = setInterval(() => {
                        action();
                        if (!_isKeyDown) {
                            clearInterval(_intervalId);
                            _intervalId = undefined;
                            console.log("claered");
                        }
                    }, interval);
                }
            }
        },
        stop(keycode) {
            if (keycode == key && document.activeElement.id.toLowerCase() !== 'chatbox') {
                _isKeyDown = false;
            }
        }
    };
}

function mouseCoord() {
    return Math.atan2(mouseY - height / 2, mouseX - width / 2);
}
function storeBuy(newHat, newAcc) {
    doNewSend(["13c", [1, newHat, 0]]);
    doNewSend(["13c", [1, newAcc, 1]]);
}
function storeEvent(newHat, newAcc) {
    if (window.location.host == "sandbox.moomoo.io" && "moomoo.io") {
        storeBuy(newHat, newAcc);
    }
    storeEquip(newHat, newAcc);
}

function storeEquip(newHat, newAcc) {
    doNewSend(["13c", [0, newHat, 0]]);
    doNewSend(["13c", [0, 0, 1]]);
    doNewSend(["13c", [0, newAcc, 1]]);
}

document.addEventListener('keyup', (e) => {
    boostSpiker.stop(e.keyCode);
    healer.stop(e.keyCode);
    Fourboost.stop(e.keyCode);
    Fourspike.stop(e.keyCode);
    if (e.keyCode == 112 && document.activeElement.id.toLowerCase() !== 'chatbox') {
        setTimeout(() => {
            send(["33", [null]]);
            boostDir = null;
        }, 10);
    }
})

function isElementVisible(e) {
    return (e.offsetParent !== null);
}

function boost() {
    for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
        ws.oldSend(getRndNumber(0, 2000000));
    }
}

function toRad(angle) {
    return angle * 0.01745329251;
}

function dist(a, b) {
    return Math.sqrt(Math.pow((b.y - a[2]), 2) + Math.pow((b.x - a[1]), 2));
}

function update() {
    for (let i = 0; i < 9; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            primary = i;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 9; i < 16; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            secondary = i;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 16; i < 19; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            foodType = i - 16;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 19; i < 22; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            wallType = i - 16;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 22; i < 26; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            spikeType = i - 16;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 26; i < 29; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            millType = i - 16;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 29; i < 31; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            mineType = i - 16;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 31; i < 33; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            boostType = i - 16;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 33; i < 39; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString())) && i != 36) {
            turretType = i - 16;
        }
    }
    spawnpadType = 36;
    for (let i = 36; i < 37; i++) {
        if (isElementVisible(document.getElementById("actionBarItem" + i.toString()))) {
            spawnpadType = i - 16;
        }
    }
}
function BullClick() {
    if (document.getElementById("spike11").checked) {
        if (animTime == 0) {
        }
        hat(animTime ==0 ? 7 : ShameCount > 3 ? (Count % 9) == 0 ? 7 : 11 : 11)
    } else {
        if (animTime == 0) {
        }
        hat(animTime == 0 ? 7 : ShameCount > 3 ? (Count % 9) == 0 ? 7 : 7 : 6)
    }
    acc(21)
}

function TankClick() {
    hat(animTime == 0 ? 40 : ShameCount > 3 ? (Count % 9) == 0 ? 7 : 26 : 6)
    acc(21)
}

function SmartClick() {
    hat(animTime == 0 ? Trapped ? 40 : isEnemyNear ? 7 : 40 : Trapped ? 26 : ShameCount > 3 ? (Count % 9) == 0 ? 7 : 26 : 26)
    acc(21)
    if (animTime == 0) {
    }
}

    }

var clickk = 0
setInterval(() => {
    if (clickk) {
        send(["c", [1]]);
        send(["c", [0]]);
    }
}, 0)

function clicking(e) {
    if (e.button == 0) {
        doNewSend(["5", [primary, true]]);
        if (click == true) {
            doClickHat = true
            clickk = 1
            LeftClick = true
            if (myPlayer.hat != 7 && myPlayer.hat != 40 && myPlayer.hat != 53) {
                Hat.doclickhat = myPlayer.hat
                Acc.doclickhat = myPlayer.accessory
            }
            if (myPlayer.weapon != 15) {
                Weapon.doclickhat = myPlayer.weapon
            }
        }
    }
    if (e.button == 2) {
        if (click == true) {
            send(["5", [secondary == 10 ? 10 : primary, true]]);
            clickk = 1
            doClickHat = true
            RightClick = true
            if (myPlayer.hat != 7 && myPlayer.hat != 40 && myPlayer.hat != 53) {
                Hat.doclickhat = myPlayer.hat
                Acc.doclickhat = myPlayer.accessory
            }
            if (myPlayer.weapon != 15) {
                Weapon.doclickhat = myPlayer.weapon
            }
        }
    }
    if (e.button == 3) {
        if (click == true) {
            clickk = 1
            doClickHat = true
            RightClick = true
            if (myPlayer.hat != 7 && myPlayer.hat != 40 && myPlayer.hat != 53) {
                Hat.doclickhat = myPlayer.hat
                Acc.doclickhat = myPlayer.accessory
            }
            if (myPlayer.weapon != 15) {
                Weapon.doclickhat = myPlayer.weapon
            }
        }
    }
}
setInterval(() => {
    if (autobs == 1) {
        if (Math.sqrt(Math.pow((myPlayer.y - EnemyInfo[2]), 2) + Math.pow((myPlayer.x - EnemyInfo[1]), 2)) < 200) {
            place(spikeType, Math.atan2(myY - myPlayer.y, myX - myPlayer.x) + toRad(0xe54324dc82));
            place(spikeType, Math.atan2(myY - myPlayer.y, myX - myPlayer.x) + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 90));
            place(spikeType, Math.atan2(myY - myPlayer.y, myX - myPlayer.x) + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 180));
            asp = 1
            send(["33", [null]]);
            setTimeout(() => {
                autobs = 0
                asp = 0
                send(["33", [null]]);
            }, 700);
            setTimeout(() => {
                send(["33", [null]]);
                send(["33", [null]]);
            }, 100);
        }
    }
}, 50)
setInterval(() => {
    if (autobs == 1) {
        if (Math.sqrt(Math.pow((myPlayer.y - EnemyInfo[2]), 2) + Math.pow((myPlayer.x - EnemyInfo[1]), 2)) > 200) {
            place(boostType, Enemycoord);
            send(["33", [Enemycoord]]);
        }
    }
}, 150)
setInterval(() => {
    if (asp == 1) {
        place(spikeType, Math.atan2(myY - myPlayer.y, myX - myPlayer.x) + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 0));
        place(spikeType, Math.atan2(myY - myPlayer.y, myX - myPlayer.x) + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 90));
        place(spikeType, Math.atan2(myY - myPlayer.y, myX - myPlayer.x) + toRad(0xe54324dc82 + 180));
    }
}, 0)

function endclick(e) {
    if (e.button == 0) {
        if (LeftClick == true) {
            doClickHat = false
            LeftClick = false
            clickk = 0
            send(["13c", [0, Hat.doclickhat, 0]]);
            send(["13c", [0, Acc.doclickhat, 1]]);
            doNewSend(["5", [primary, true]]);
        }
    }
    if (e.button == 2) {
        if (RightClick == true) {
            clickk = 0
            doClickHat = false
            send(["5", [primary, true]]);
            RightClick = false
            send(["13c", [0, Hat.doclickhat, 0]]);
            send(["13c", [0, Acc.doclickhat, 1]]);
        }
    }
    if (e.button == 3) {
        if (RightClick == true) {
            clickk = 0
            doClickHat = false
            RightClick = false
            send(["13c", [0, Hat.doclickhat, 0]]);
            send(["13c", [0, Acc.doclickhat, 1]]);
        }
    }
}
setInterval(() => {
    if (doClickHat && !ProcessInsta && !Breaking) {
        if (RightClick && !LeftClick) {
            TankClick()
            send(["c", [1]]);
            send(["c", [null]]);
            send(["2", [Math.atan2(mouseY - height / 2, mouseX - width / 2)]]);
        }
        if (!RightClick && LeftClick) {
            BullClick()
            send(["c", [1]]);
            send(["c", [null]]);
            send(["2", [Math.atan2(mouseY - height / 2, mouseX - width / 2)]]);
        }
        if (RightClick && LeftClick) {
            send(["2", [Math.atan2(mouseY - height / 2, mouseX - width / 2)]]);
            SmartClick()
            send(["c", [1]]);
            send(["c", [null]]);
        }
    }
}, 25);

                function PL(e, t) {
                    e = e / (Math.PI / 180);
                    let ang = null; //Math.PI , i += Math.PI/8
                    for (let i = -180; i < 180; i += 22.5) {
                        if (e == i) {
                            i < 0 && (i += 360);
                            let a = i / 22.5;
                            ang = ia[a];
                        }

                function oP(x, y) {
                    let a = Math.atan2(y - nEy[2], x - nEy[1]),
                        b = Math.atan2(y - R.y2, x - R.x2);
                    let c = (b += Math.PI / 2.5);
                    let d = (b -= Math.PI / 2.5);
                    c > Math.PI * 2 && (c -= Math.PI * 2);
                    d > Math.PI * 2 && (d -= Math.PI * 2);
                    c < 0 && (c += Math.PI * 2 + a);
                    d < 0 && (d += Math.PI * 2 + b);
                    if (c > a && d < a) {
                        return true;
                    } else if (d > 290 && a < 70 && c < a + Math.PI / 2.4) {
                        return true;
                    } else if (a > 290 && d > a - Math.PI / 2.6 && c < Math.PI / 2.45) {
                        return true;
                    } else {
                        return false;
                    }
                    /*if((nEA+Math.PI/2.5) > a && (nEA-Math.PI/2.5) < a){
            return true
        }else{
            return false
        }*/
                }

                function Fn(e, t, n, i) {
                    be.save(),
                        be.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0),
                        be.scale(V, V);
                    var r = 50;
                    be.beginPath(),
                        be.arc(e, t, r, 0, 2 * Math.PI, !1),
                        be.closePath(),
                        be.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)",
                        be.fill(),
                        r = 50;
                    var s = n - e
                    , a = i - t
                    , o = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(s, 2) + Math.pow(a, 2))
                    , c = o > r ? o / r : 1;
                    s /= c,
                        a /= c,
                        be.beginPath(),
                        be.arc(e + s, t + a, .5 * r, 0, 2 * Math.PI, !1),
                        be.closePath(),
                        be.fillStyle = "white",
                        be.fill(),
                        be.restore()
                }

                function ai(e, t, n, i) {

                }

                function setAdvCooldown(e, t, n, i, r){
                    let min = Infinity;
                    let id = -1;
                    for(let i = 0; i < W.length;i++){
                        (_ = W[i]) && _.visible && _.secondary && l.weapons[_.secondary].projectile !== undefined && l.projectiles[l.weapons[_.secondary].projectile].speed == r &&
                            min > (_.x2-e+Math.cos(n)*70)**2+(_.y2-t+Math.sin(n)*70)**2
                        && (id = _.sid, min = (_.x2-e+Math.cos(n)*70)**2+(_.y2-t+Math.sin(n)*70)**2)
                    }
                    if(Math.sqrt(min) > 80){
                        if(r == 1.5){
                            for(let i = 0; i < W.length;i++){
                                (_ = W[i]) && _.visible &&
                                    min > (_.x2-e)**2+(_.y2-t)**2
                                && (id = _.sid, min = (_.x2-e)**2+(_.y2-t)**2)
                            }
                            if(Math.sqrt(min) < 60){
                                setTimeout(()=>{turretReload[id] = 0});
                            }
                        }else{
                            for(let i = 0; i < W.length;i++){
                                (_ = W[i]) && _.visible && _.secondary &&
                                    min > (_.x2-e+Math.cos(n)*70)**2+(_.y2-t+Math.sin(n)*70)**2
                                && (id = _.sid, min = (_.x2-e+Math.cos(n)*70)**2+(_.y2-t+Math.sin(n)*70)**2)
                            }
                            _=Ii(id);
                            setTimeout(()=>{secondaryReload[id] = 0});
                        }
                    }else{
                        _=Ii(id);
                        setTimeout(()=>{secondaryReload[id] = 0});
                    }
                }

                    }));

                },

                },

                                var t = Math.abs(e.x - this.x) - e.scale,
                                    n = Math.abs(e.y - this.y) - e.scale;
                                return t <= a.maxScreenWidth / 2 * 1.3 && n <= a.maxScreenHeight / 2 * 1.3
                            };
                            var h = 0,
                                u = 0;
                            this.animate = function (e) {
                                this.animTime > 0 && (this.animTime -= e, this.animTime <= 0 ? (this.animTime = 0, this.dirPlus = 0, h = 0, u = 0) : 0 == u ? (h += e / (this.animSpeed * a.hitReturnRatio), this.dirPlus = s.lerp(0, this.targetAngle, Math.min(1, h)), h >= 1 && (h = 1, u = 1)) : (h -= e / (this.animSpeed * (1 - a.hitReturnRatio)), this.dirPlus = s.lerp(0, this.targetAngle, Math.max(0, h))))
                            },
                                this.startAnim = function () {
                                this.animTime = this.animSpeed = 600,
                                    this.targetAngle = .8 * Math.PI,
                                    h = 0,
                                    u = 0
                            },
                                this.changeHealth = function (e, t, n) {
                                if (this.active && (this.health += e, n && (this.hitScare && !s.randInt(0, this.hitScare) ? (this.runFrom = n, this.waitCount = 0, this.moveCount = 2e3) : this.hostile && this.chargePlayer && n.isPlayer ? (this.chargeTarget = n, this.waitCount = 0, this.moveCount = 8e3) : this.dontRun || (this.runFrom = n, this.waitCount = 0, this.moveCount = 2e3)), e < 0 && this.hitRange && s.randInt(0, 1) && (this.hitWait = 500), t && t.canSee(this) && e < 0 && c.send(t.id, "t", Math.round(this.x), Math.round(this.y), Math.round(-e), 1), this.health <= 0 && (this.spawnDelay ? (this.spawnCounter = this.spawnDelay, this.x = -1e6, this.y = -1e6) : (this.x = this.startX || s.randInt(0, a.mapScale), this.y = this.startY || s.randInt(0, a.mapScale)), this.health = this.maxHealth, this.runFrom = null, t && (o(t, this.killScore), this.drop))))
                                    for (var i = 0; i < this.drop.length;) t.addResource(a.resourceTypes.indexOf(this.drop[i]), this.drop[i + 1]),
                                        i += 2
                            }
                        }
                    }]);

(function () {
    var UPDATE_DELAY = 700;
    var lastUpdate = 0;
    var frames = 0;
    var values;

    function updateCounter() {
        var now = Date.now();
        var elapsed = now - lastUpdate;
        if (elapsed < UPDATE_DELAY) {
            ++frames;
        } else {
            var fps = Math.round(frames / (elapsed / 1000));
            document.getElementById("fps").textContent = "Fps: " + fps;
            frames = 0;
            lastUpdate = now;
        }
        requestAnimationFrame(updateCounter);
    }
    lastUpdate = Date.now();
    requestAnimationFrame(updateCounter);
})();

var kills = 10

function getkills() {
    var count = parseInt(document.getElementById("killCounter").innerText);
    if (count > kills) {
        chat("HA? = " + count+" kills!");
    }
    kills = count;
}

// Get modal element
var modal = document.getElementById("simpleModal");
// Get close button
var closeBtn = document.getElementsByClassName('closeBtn')[0];
// Events
closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
window.addEventListener('click', outsideClick);
// Close
function closeModal() {
    modal.style.display = 'none';
}
// Close If Outside Click
function outsideClick(e) {
    if (e.target == modal) {
        modal.style.display = 'none';
    }
}
